<t>CREATE TABLE Game ( game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255), genre VARCHAR(50), release_date DATE, platform VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE Player ( player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), email VARCHAR(255), date_of_birth DATE, country VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE Scoreboard ( game_id INT, player_id INT, score INT, level INT, PRIMARY KEY (game_id, player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>UPDATE Game SET genre='Action' WHERE title='Mario Kart';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE Game ( game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255), genre VARCHAR(50), release_date DATE, platform VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE Player ( player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), email VARCHAR(255), date_of_birth DATE, country VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE Scoreboard ( game_id INT, player_id INT, score INT, level INT, PRIMARY KEY (game_id, player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>update game set genre='action' where title='mario kart';</s>

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE Scoreboard ( game_id INT, player_id INT, score INT, level INT, PRIMARY KEY (game_id, player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE Player ( player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), email VARCHAR(255), date_of_birth DATE, country VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>UPDATE Game SET genre='Action' WHERE title='Mario Kart';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE Game ( game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255), genre VARCHAR(50), release_date DATE, platform VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE Scoreboard ( game_id INT, player_id INT, score INT, level INT, PRIMARY KEY (game_id, player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE Player ( player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), email VARCHAR(255), date_of_birth DATE, country VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>update game set genre='action' where title='mario kart';</s>

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE Player ( player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), email VARCHAR(255), date_of_birth DATE, country VARCHAR(50) );</t><s>UPDATE Scoreboard SET score=500 WHERE game_id=1 AND player_id=1;</s>

CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));

CREATE TABLE GameReview (ReviewID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameID INT, PlayerID INT, Rating INT, ReviewText TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID), FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));</t><s>update player set age = 25 where playerid = 1;</s>

CREATE TABLE Game (GameID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameName VARCHAR(50), ReleaseDate DATE, Genre VARCHAR(50), Platform VARCHAR(50);</t><s>UPDATE Game SET Genre = 'Action' WHERE GameID = 1;</s>
